%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\Section{{LM}}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\Link[http://www.tug.org/texlive/Contents/live/texmf-dist/doc/fonts/lm/lm-info.pdf]{}{}http://www.tug.org/texlive/Contents/live/texmf-dist/doc/fonts/lm/lm-info.pdf\EndLink


\Verbatim
Package: Latin Modern fonts
Authors: JNSteam
License: GUST Font Source License
Location on CTAN: fonts/lm

The Latin Modern family of fonts is based on the Computer Modern fonts
in the PostScript Type 1 format, released into public domain by the
American Mathematical Society. The fonts, as compared to the CM family,
contain a lot of additional characters, mainly accented ones, but not only.
The current distribution contains:
Latin Modern fonts in the PostScript Type 1 and OpenType formats,
source files for MetaType1 plus all requisites for using the fonts with
TeX/pdfTeX; there is one set of PostScript fonts and five sets of TeX Font
Metric files, corresponding to:
-- EC (Cork) encoding (ec-*.tfm),
-- QX encoding (qx-*.tfm),
-- TeX'n'ANSI aka LY1 encoding (texnansi-*.tfm),
-- T5 (Vietnamese) encoding (t5-*.tfm),
-- Text Companion for EC fonts aka TS1 (ts1-*.tfm).
\EndVerbatim





%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\Section{lm}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%

                    Eitan M. Gurari >>>

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\SubSection{SUB: Vn}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


The vn.htf font was originally created for the vnr (vietnamese Computer
Modern) fonts. Then because the urwvn fonts use the same encoding, 
 those aliases for urwvn got created.


\<vn-uni\><<<
.lm-rep-t5psn
htfcss: vnb     font-weight: bold;
htfcss: vnbi    font-weight: bold;  font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnbl    font-weight: bold;  font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnbx    font-weight: bold;
htfcss: vnbxsl  font-style: oblique; font-weight: bold;
htfcss: vnbxti  font-weight: bold;  font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnfi    font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnfs    font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnit    font-style: italic;  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnitt   font-style: italic;  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnqi    font-style: italic;  font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vnrb    font-weight: bold;
htfcss: vnsi    font-style: italic;  font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vnsl    font-style: italic;
htfcss: vnsl  font-style: oblique;
htfcss: vnsltt  font-style: italic;  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnso    font-weight: bold;  font-style:italic; font-family:sans-serif;
htfcss: vnss    font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vnssbx  font-family: sans-serif; font-weight: bold;
htfcss: vnssdc  font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vnssi  font-family: sans-serif; font-style: oblique;
htfcss: vnssq  font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vnssqi  font-family: sans-serif; font-style: oblique;
htfcss: vnst    font-style: italic;  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnsx    font-weight: bold;  font-family: sans-serif;
htfcss: vntc    font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vntcsc  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnti    font-style: italic;
htfcss: vntt    font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnu  font-style: oblique; font-style:italic;
htfcss: vnvi    font-style: italic;  font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnvt    font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnvtt   font-family: monospace;
htfcss: vnxc    font-weight: bold;
>>>

\def\;{`}
\def\!{>>>}

\<non kurier calling macros\><<<
`<main macros`>      
`<extract htfcss`>

\def\xmap#1{
  \def\act##1{
     \edef\one{\par}\edef\two{##1}\ifx \one\two \else
        `<xmap css`>%
        \expandafter \ifx\csname \file.\alias.\check\endcsname\relax
                \expandafter \let\csname \file.\alias.\check\endcsname=\def
           \ifx \check\empty
              \ifx \file\alias\else
                    \immediate\write16{\string\<\file\NEW\string\><<<}
                    \immediate\write16{.\alias }
                    \immediate\write16{`!}
                    \immediate\write16{\string\AddFont{\file\NEW}{alias/\FAM/\alias/\file}}
              \fi 
           \else
              \ifx \file\alias
                 \immediate\write16{\string\<htfcss \alias\string\><<<}
                 \immediate\write16{htfcss: \file \space \check}
                 \immediate\write16{`!}
              \else
                 \immediate\write16{\string\<\file\NEW\string\><<<}
                 \immediate\write16{.\alias }
                 \immediate\write16{htfcss: \file \space \check}
                 \immediate\write16{`!}
                 \immediate\write16{\string\AddFont{\file\NEW}{alias/\FAM/\alias/\file}}
           \fi \fi
        \fi \fi
     \fi
  }
  \readfile{#1.map}
}

\def\defkey#1{%
   \ifnum \c < 0  
       \if !#1! \advance\c by -1 \fi
   \fi
   \def\key{#1}%
   \def\SYN{}%
   \expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\modkey
       \expandafter\string\csname #1.\endcsname//%
}
\def\temp#1{\def\modkey##1##2}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter  \temp
      \expandafter\string\csname .\endcsname#3//{
   \if !#3!%     
   \else
      \expandafter\ifx \csname \key\endcsname\relax
         \def\key{#2 }% 
         \def\SYN{*}
      \fi
   \fi
}

\newcount\c
\newcount\linec

\def\xenc#1{
  \def\act##1{
     \edef\one{\par}\edef\two{##1}\ifx \one\two \else
        \def\check{}
        \defkey{##1}%
        \expandafter \ifx \csname \key\endcsname\relax
           \ifnum\c>-1 \ifnum\c<256
              \immediate\write16{............=##1=      \the\c}
           \fi \fi   
        \else
           \ifnum  \c<\startat \relax \else
           \ifnum  \c>\endat   \relax \else
              \advance\linec by 1
              \immediate\write16{'\csname \key\endcsname'  
                  '\expandafter\ifx \csname \key 2\endcsname\relax \else
                        \csname ##12\endcsname
                   \fi ' 
                  \expandafter\ifx \csname ##13\endcsname\relax
                        \% ##1 \%
                  \else 
                      \expandafter\ifx \csname ##13\endcsname\empty\else
                       \%\csname ##13\endcsname\%
                      \fi
                  \fi
                  \space
                   \SYN\the\c\space
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\ifcase \c
`;<v 2005`;>
\or `;<c gurari 2005`;>
\or `;<version 2`;> 
\or `;<version 3`;> 
\or `;<version 4`;> 
\or `;<version 5`;> 
\or `;<version 6`;> 
\or `;<version 7`;>  
\or `;<version 8`;> 
\or `;<version 9`;> 
\or `;<version 10`;> 
\or `;<version 11`;> 
\or `;<version 12`;>  
\or `;<version 13`;> 
\or `;<version 14`;> 
\or `;<version 15`;> 
\or `;<version 16`;> 
\or `;<version 17`;> 
\or `;<version 18`;> 
\else
\fi
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
           }
        \fi \fi \fi
        \advance\c by 1
     \fi
  }
  \c=-1
  \linec=-1
  \immediate\write16{\string\<#1\NEW\string\><<<}
  \immediate\write16{#1 \startat\space \endat}
  \readfile{#1.enc}
  \immediate\write16{#1 \startat\space \endat}
  \immediate\write16{`;<htfcss #1`;>}
  \immediate\write16{`!}
  \immediate\write16{\string\<htfcss #1\string\><<<}
  \immediate\write16{`!}
  \AtEndDocument{\immediate\write16{\string\AddFont{#1\NEW}{unicode/\FAM/#1}}}
  \immediate\write16{}
}
`<DEF`>
>>>





\<kurier calling macros\><<<
`<main macros`>   
`<extract htfcss`>

\def\xmap#1{
  \def\act##1{
     \edef\one{\par}\edef\two{##1}\ifx \one\two \else
        `<xmap css`>
        \let\savealias=\alias
        \expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dofix
                  \expandafter\string\csname\alias\endcsname//
        \expandafter \ifx\csname \file.\savealias.\check\endcsname\relax
                \expandafter \let\csname \file.\savealias.\check\endcsname=\def
           \expandafter \ifx\csname \file+\endcsname\relax
                \expandafter \let\csname \file+\endcsname=\def
                 \immediate\write16{\string\<\file\NEW\string\><<<}
                 \immediate\write16{.\alias }
                 \immediate\write16{`;<htfcss \file`;>}
                 \immediate\write16{`!}
               \edef\temp{\noexpand
                 \AtEndDocument{\noexpand\immediate\write16{\string\AddFont{\file\NEW}}}
                 \noexpand\AtEndDocument{\noexpand\immediate\write16{{alias/\FAM/\alias/\file}}}}
               \temp
              \immediate\write16{\string\<htfcss \file\string\><<<}
                 \immediate\write16{`!}
           \fi      
                  \ifx \check\empty\else
                 \immediate\write16{\string\<htfcss \file\string\><<<}
                 \immediate\write16{htfcss: \file \space \check}
                 \immediate\write16{`!}
           \fi 
        \fi
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\expandafter \ifx\csname \savealias+\endcsname\relax
     \expandafter \let\csname \savealias+\endcsname=\def
      \immediate\write16{\string\<\savealias\NEW\string\><<<}
      \immediate\write16{.\alias }
      \immediate\write16{`;<htfcss \savealias`;>}
      \immediate\write16{`!}
      \edef\temp{\noexpand\AtEndDocument{
              \noexpand\immediate
              \write16{\string\AddFont{\savealias\NEW}}
              \noexpand\immediate
              \write16{{alias/\FAM/\alias/\savealias}}
      }}\temp
      \immediate\write16{\string\<htfcss \savealias\string\><<<}
      \immediate\write16{`!}
\fi
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
     \fi
  }
  \readfile{#1.map}
}

\def\FIX#1{\def\fix##1}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\FIX
     \expandafter\string\csname \FAM\endcsname#2//{\def\alias{#1iwona#2}}

\def\dofix#1{\fix}
>>>


\<main macros\><<<
\def\xx#1#2{%
    \def\startat{#1}
    \def\endat{#2}
    \x
   }

\def\x#1.#2.{%
   \csname x#2\endcsname{#1}}

\def\readfile#1{
   \immediate\openin15=#1
   \readrec
}
\def\readrec{
   \ifeof15 
      \immediate\closein15
   \else
      \immediate\read15 to \rec
      \act\rec
      \expandafter \readrec
   \fi
}

\def\trim#1//{
   \let\first=\empty \let\second\empty
   \decomp#1//%
   \edef\file{\first \second}%
}

\def\decomp#1#2//{%
  \if !#2!%
     \let\next\empty
     \def\second{#1}%
     \ifnum 10=1\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 1=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 2=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 3=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 4=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 5=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 6=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 7=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 8=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifnum 9=0\second \edef\next{\noexpand\decomp\first//}\fi
     \ifx \next\empty\else
        \let\first=\empty \let\second\empty
     \fi
  \else 
     \edef\first{\first#1}   
     \def\next{\decomp#2//}
  \fi
  \next
}

\def\checkalias #1 #2<#3.#4//{\def\alias{#3}\def\file{#1}}

{ 
\catcode`;\%=12 
\gdef\%{ `;% } 
\gdef\COM{% } 
} 
>>>

\<extract htfcss\><<<
\def\dochechbf#1{\chechbf}
\def\chechbf#1{\def\chechbf##1}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechbf
\expandafter\string \csname Bold\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-weight: bold;\check}\fi}

\def\dochechhl#1{\chechhl}
\def\chechhl#1{\def\chechhl##1}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechhl
\expandafter\string \csname Heavy\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-weight: bold;\check}\fi}

\def\dochechit#1{\chechit}
\def\chechit#1{\def\chechit##1}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechit
\expandafter\string \csname Italic\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-style:italic;\check}\fi}

\def\dochechtt#1{\chechtt}
\def\chechtt#1{\def\chechtt##1}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechtt
\expandafter\string \csname Typewriter\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-family: monospace;\check}\fi}

\def\dochechob#1{\chechob}

\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechob
\expandafter\string \csname Oblique\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-style: oblique;\check}\fi}

\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechsans
\expandafter\string \csname Sans\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-family: sans-serif;\check}\fi}

\def\dochechli#1{\chechli}

\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\chechmo
\expandafter\string \csname Mono\endcsname#2//{\if !#2!\else
    \edef\check{ font-family: monospace;\check}\fi}

\<xmap css\><<<
\def\check{}
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechbf 
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Bold\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechhl 
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Heavy\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechit
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Italic\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechtt
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Typewriter\endcsname//

   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Oblique\endcsname//

   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Sans\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechli
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Light\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechsl
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Slant\endcsname//
\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\dochechmo
   \expandafter\string\csname ##1Mono\endcsname//
\ifx \rec\empty \else
\expandafter\checkalias ##1<.//
\ifx \file\alias \else
    \expandafter\trim \file//
\fi

\<DEF\><<<
\def\DEF#1{%
   \expandafter\gdef\csname /#1\endcsname
}

\catcode`;\_=12
\catcode`;\~=12
\catcode`;\^=12

\DEF{.notdef }{} \DEF{.notdef 3}{}
